mw-body-content">\n\t</div>\n\t<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Comparison of feed aggregators</h1>\n\t<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">\n\t\t<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>\n\t\t<div id="contentSub"></div>\n\t\t<div id="contentSub2"></div>\n\t\t\n\t\t<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>\n\t\t<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>\n\t\t<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>\n\t\t<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table class="box-Update plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="Ambox current red Americas.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Ambox_current_red_Americas.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red_Americas.svg.png" decoding="async" width="42" height="34" class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">The <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Accuracy_dispute" title="Wikipedia:Accuracy dispute">factual accuracy</a></b> of parts of this article (those related to article) <b>may be compromised due to out-of-date information</b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">March 2013</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>The following is a <b>comparison of RSS feed aggregators</b>. Often e-mail programs and web browsers have the ability to display <a href="/wiki/RSS" title="RSS">RSS</a> feeds. They are listed here, too.\n</p><p>Many <a href="/wiki/BitTorrent_client" class="mw-redirect" title="BitTorrent client">BitTorrent clients</a> support RSS feeds for <a href="/wiki/Broadcatching" title="Broadcatching">broadcatching</a> (see <a href="/wiki/Comparison_of_BitTorrent_clients" title="Comparison of BitTorrent clients">Comparison of BitTorrent clients</a>).\n</p><p>With the rise of <a href="/wiki/Cloud_computing" title="Cloud computing">cloud computing</a>, some cloud based services offer <a href="/wiki/Feed_aggregator" class="mw-redirect" title="Feed aggregator">feed aggregation</a>. They are listed here as well.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox"
